34: 
35: ```
36: 1. Open dashboard → everything green, 0 attacks
37: 
38: 2. Sidebar → Attack Type = SQLi → Launch Attack
39:    → Dashboard flashes red
40:    → Log: CRITICAL | SQLi | 192.168.1.100 | BLOCKED
41:    → Confidence: 75%
42: 
43: 3. Click CVE tab → CVE-2023-23752 card pulls up
44:    → CVSS 9.8 CRITICAL | "This attack = trending globally"
45: 
46: 4. Payload Inspector → shows raw SQL injection string
47:    → Auto-Defense: "Parameterized queries applied. IP DROPPED"

50:    → Metric row counts up live
51: 
52: 6. Clear → everything green again
53:    → "System healed."
54: ```
55:

57: 
58: ## Architecture
59: 
60: ```
61: Attacker (attack_simulator.py)
62:         ↓  HTTP requests with SQLi/XSS/LFI/CMDi payloads
63: Scapy engine (scapy_engine.py)
64:         ↓  Packet sniff → decode → regex + rule engine
65: Attack Detector
66:         ↓  attack_type, severity, confidence, CVE hint
67: Auto Blocker (auto_block.py)
68:         ↓  iptables DROP rule (or in-memory for demo)
69: Dashboard (dashboard.py)
70:         ↓  Real-time log, CVE card, payload inspector
71: NVD API (cve_lookup.py)
72:         ↓  Live CVE data with CVSS scores
73: ```
74: 
75: ---
76: 
77: ## File Guide
78: 
79: | File | What it does |
80: |------|-------------|
81: | `scapy_engine.py` | Packet sniffer + multi-type attack classifier (SQLi/XSS/LFI/CMDi). Runs `simulate_attack()` without root. |
82: | `auto_block.py` | `BlockManager` — fires iptables, tracks rates, auto-expires blocks after 1 hour. |
83: | `cve_lookup.py` | NVD API wrapper with fallback static data. `get_cve_card(attack_type)` for dashboard. |
84: | `attack_simulator.py` | Fires real HTTP payloads at `localhost:8080`. CLI: `python attack_simulator.py --type SQLi` |
85: | `dashboard.py` | Full Streamlit UI: metrics, live log, CVE panel, payload inspector. |
86: 
87: ---

90: 
91: ```bash
92: # Start test web server (victim)
93: python -m http.server 8080
94: 
95: # Fire attacks from another terminal
96: python attack_simulator.py --type SQLi --target http://localhost:8080
97: 
98: # Run engine with root (sniff mode)
99: sudo python scapy_engine.py
100: ```

<content>
1: """
2: AutoShield - Scapy Traffic Capture + Attack Detection Engine
3: Intercepts HTTP traffic, classifies SQLi/XSS/LFI attacks via rule engine + ML
4: """
5: 
6: import re
7: import json
8: import time
9: import threading
10: import logging
11: from datetime import datetime
12: from collections import defaultdict
13: from urllib.parse import unquote_plus
14: 
15: # Scapy imports (graceful fallback for non-root dev mode)
16: try:
17:     from scapy.all import sniff, TCP, IP, Raw
18:     SCAPY_AVAILABLE = True
19: except ImportError:
20:     SCAPY_AVAILABLE = False
21:     print("[WARNING] Scapy not available. Running in simulation mode.")
22: 
23: logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(message)s')
24: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.Engine")
25: 
26: # ─── Attack Signature Rules ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
27: 
28: SQLI_PATTERNS = [
29:     r"(?i)(union\s+select)",
30:     r"(?i)(select\s+.*\s+from)",
31:     r"(?i)(insert\s+into)",
32:     r"(?i)(drop\s+table)",
33:     r"(?i)(exec\s*\(|execute\s*\()",
34:     r"(?i)(--\s*$|;\s*--)",
35:     r"(?i)(\bor\b\s+['\"]?\d+['\"]?\s*=\s*['\"]?\d+['\"]?)",
36:     r"(?i)(sleep\s*\(\s*\d+\s*\))",
37:     r"(?i)(benchmark\s*\()",
38:     r"(?i)(information_schema)",
39:     r"(?i)(load_file\s*\()",
40:     r"(?i)(into\s+outfile)",
41:     r"'[^']*'[^']*=",
42:     r"(?i)(xp_cmdshell)",
43:     r"(?i)(waitfor\s+delay)",
44: ]
45: 
46: XSS_PATTERNS = [
47:     r"(?i)<script[^>]*>",
48:     r"(?i)</script>",
49:     r"(?i)(javascript\s*:)",
50:     r"(?i)(on\w+\s*=\s*['\"])",
51:     r"(?i)(alert\s*\()",
52:     r"(?i)(document\.cookie)",
53:     r"(?i)(document\.write\s*\()",
54:     r"(?i)(eval\s*\()",
55:     r"(?i)(<iframe[^>]*>)",
56:     r"(?i)(src\s*=\s*['\"]javascript:)",
57:     r"(?i)(vbscript\s*:)",
58:     r"(?i)(<img[^>]+onerror\s*=)",
59:     r"(?i)(\.innerHTML\s*=)",
60:     r"(?i)(fromcharcode)",
61:     r"(?i)(&#x[0-9a-f]+;)",
62: ]
63: 
64: LFI_PATTERNS = [
65:     r"(\.\.\/){2,}",
66:     r"(\.\.\\){2,}",
67:     r"(?i)(\/etc\/passwd)",
68:     r"(?i)(\/etc\/shadow)",
69:     r"(?i)(\/proc\/self)",
70:     r"(?i)(\/windows\/system32)",
71:     r"(?i)(boot\.ini)",
72:     r"(?i)(php:\/\/filter)",
73:     r"(?i)(php:\/\/input)",
74:     r"(?i)(data:\/\/text)",
75:     r"(?i)(expect:\/\/)",
76:     r"(?i)(\.\.[\/\\]){1,}(etc|windows|proc)",
77:     r"(?i)(\/var\/log)",
78:     r"(?i)(file:\/\/\/)",
79: ]
80: 
81: CMDI_PATTERNS = [
82:     r"(?i)(;[\s]*ls\b)",
83:     r"(?i)(;[\s]*cat\b)",
84:     r"(?i)(\|[\s]*(ls|cat|id|whoami|pwd|uname))",
85:     r"(?i)(`[\s]*(ls|cat|id|whoami)[\s]*`)",
86:     r"(?i)(\$\([\s]*(id|whoami|ls)[\s]*\))",
87:     r"(?i)(nc\s+-[lne]+\s+\d+)",
88:     r"(?i)(curl\s+http)",
89:     r"(?i)(wget\s+http)",
90:     r"(?i)(chmod\s+[0-7]{3,4})",
91:     r"(?i)(rm\s+-rf)",
92: ]
93: 
94: ATTACK_RULES = {
95:     "SQLi":  SQLI_PATTERNS,
96:     "XSS":   XSS_PATTERNS,
97:     "LFI":   LFI_PATTERNS,
98:     "CMDi":  CMDI_PATTERNS,
99: }
100: 
101: SEVERITY_MAP = {
102:     "SQLi": "CRITICAL",
103:     "XSS":  "HIGH",
104:     "LFI":  "CRITICAL",
105:     "CMDi": "CRITICAL",
106: }
107: 
108: # CVE mappings for common patterns (demo-ready)
109: CVE_HINT_MAP = {
110:     "SQLi": ["CVE-2023-23752", "CVE-2023-28343", "CVE-2023-0179"],
111:     "XSS":  ["CVE-2023-32315", "CVE-2023-24044", "CVE-2023-33225"],
112:     "LFI":  ["CVE-2023-29489", "CVE-2023-27035", "CVE-2023-25157"],
113:     "CMDi": ["CVE-2023-44487", "CVE-2023-28434", "CVE-2023-46604"],
114: }
115: 
116: # ─── Detection Engine ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
117: 
118: class AttackDetector:
119:     def __init__(self):
120:         self.compiled_rules = {
121:             atype: [re.compile(p) for p in patterns]
122:             for atype, patterns in ATTACK_RULES.items()
123:         }
124:         self.stats = defaultdict(int)
125: 
126:     def classify(self, payload: str) -> dict | None:
127:         """
128:         Returns attack dict if malicious payload detected, else None.
129:         Multi-rule match → highest-severity type returned.
130:         """
131:         decoded = unquote_plus(payload)
132:         matches = {}
133: 
134:         for atype, patterns in self.compiled_rules.items():
135:             hits = [p.pattern for p in patterns if p.search(decoded)]
136:             if hits:
137:                 matches[atype] = hits
138: 
139:         if not matches:
140:             return None
141: 
142:         # Priority: CMDi > SQLi > LFI > XSS
143:         priority = ["CMDi", "SQLi", "LFI", "XSS"]
144:         attack_type = next((t for t in priority if t in matches), list(matches.keys())[0])
145: 
146:         self.stats[attack_type] += 1
147: 
148:         return {
149:             "attack_type":  attack_type,
150:             "severity":     SEVERITY_MAP[attack_type],
151:             "matched_rules": matches[attack_type][:3],   # top 3 matched
152:             "cve_hints":    CVE_HINT_MAP[attack_type],
153:             "payload_snip": decoded[:200],
154:             "confidence":   min(100, len(matches[attack_type]) * 25),
155:         }
156: 
157: 
158: # ─── Packet Sniffer ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
159: 
160: class AutoShieldEngine:
161:     def __init__(self, interface="eth0", port=80, event_callback=None):
162:         self.interface      = interface
163:         self.port           = port
164:         self.event_callback = event_callback  # fn(event_dict) called on detection
165:         self.detector       = AttackDetector()
166:         self.running        = False
167:         self._thread        = None
168:         self.attack_log     = []
169:         self._lock          = threading.Lock()
170: 
171:     # ── packet handler ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
172:     def _process_packet(self, packet):
173:         if not (packet.haslayer(TCP) and packet.haslayer(Raw) and packet.haslayer(IP)):
174:             return
175: 
176:         raw_data = packet[Raw].load.decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
177: 
178:         # Extract HTTP request line + body
179:         if not any(m in raw_data for m in ["GET ", "POST ", "PUT ", "DELETE "]):
180:             return
181: 
182:         src_ip  = packet[IP].src
183:         dst_ip  = packet[IP].dst
184:         dst_port = packet[TCP].dport
185: 
186:         # Pull URL + body for analysis
187:         lines  = raw_data.split("\r\n")
188:         target = raw_data   # full request as payload
189: 
190:         result = self.detector.classify(target)
191:         if not result:
192:             return
193: 
194:         event = {
195:             "timestamp":   datetime.now().isoformat(),
196:             "src_ip":      src_ip,
197:             "dst_ip":      dst_ip,
198:             "dst_port":    dst_port,
199:             "attack_type": result["attack_type"],
200:             "severity":    result["severity"],
201:             "confidence":  result["confidence"],
202:             "cve_hints":   result["cve_hints"],
203:             "payload_snip": result["payload_snip"],
204:             "matched_rules": result["matched_rules"],
205:             "action":      "PENDING",
206:             "status":      "DETECTED",
207:         }
208: 
209:         with self._lock:
210:             self.attack_log.append(event)
211: 
212:         log.warning(
213:             f"[{result['severity']}] {result['attack_type']} from {src_ip} "
214:             f"| confidence={result['confidence']}% | CVE hint: {result['cve_hints'][0]}"
215:         )
216: 
217:         if self.event_callback:
218:             self.event_callback(event)
219: 
220:     # ── start / stop ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
221:     def start(self):
222:         if not SCAPY_AVAILABLE:
223:             log.warning("Scapy unavailable. Use simulate_attack() for demo.")
224:             return
225: 
226:         self.running = True
227:         self._thread = threading.Thread(target=self._sniff_loop, daemon=True)
228:         self._thread.start()
229:         log.info(f"Engine started on {self.interface}:{self.port}")
230: 
231:     def _sniff_loop(self):
232:         sniff(
233:             iface=self.interface,
234:             filter=f"tcp port {self.port}",
235:             prn=self._process_packet,
236:             store=False,
237:             stop_filter=lambda _: not self.running,
238:         )
239: 
240:     def stop(self):
241:         self.running = False
242:         log.info("Engine stopped.")
243: 
244:     # ── simulation mode (demo / testing) ────────────────────────────────────
245:     def simulate_attack(self, attack_type: str = "SQLi", src_ip: str = "192.168.1.66"):
246:         """Inject a fake attack event — for demo without root/Scapy."""
247:         DEMO_PAYLOADS = {
248:             "SQLi": "GET /login?user=' OR 1=1 -- &pass=x HTTP/1.1",
249:             "XSS":  "GET /search?q=<script>alert(document.cookie)</script> HTTP/1.1",
250:             "LFI":  "GET /page?file=../../../../etc/passwd HTTP/1.1",
251:             "CMDi": "GET /ping?host=8.8.8.8;cat /etc/shadow HTTP/1.1",
252:         }
253:         payload = DEMO_PAYLOADS.get(attack_type, DEMO_PAYLOADS["SQLi"])
254:         result  = self.detector.classify(payload)
255:         if not result:
256:             return None
257: 
258:         event = {
259:             "timestamp":    datetime.now().isoformat(),
260:             "src_ip":       src_ip,
261:             "dst_ip":       "10.0.0.1",
262:             "dst_port":     80,
263:             "attack_type":  result["attack_type"],
264:             "severity":     result["severity"],
265:             "confidence":   result["confidence"],
266:             "cve_hints":    result["cve_hints"],
267:             "payload_snip": payload,
268:             "matched_rules": result["matched_rules"],
269:             "action":       "PENDING",
270:             "status":       "DETECTED",
271:         }
272: 
273:         with self._lock:
274:             self.attack_log.append(event)
275: 
276:         if self.event_callback:
277:             self.event_callback(event)
278: 
279:         return event
280: 
281:     def get_log(self):
282:         with self._lock:
283:             return list(self.attack_log)
284: 
285:     def mark_blocked(self, src_ip: str):
286:         with self._lock:
287:             for e in self.attack_log:
288:                 if e["src_ip"] == src_ip and e["action"] == "PENDING":
289:                     e["action"] = "BLOCKED"
290:                     e["status"] = "MITIGATED"
291: 
292: 
293: # ─── Quick test ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
294: 
295: if __name__ == "__main__":
296:     def on_attack(event):
297:         print(f"\n🚨 ATTACK DETECTED: {event['attack_type']} from {event['src_ip']}")
298:         print(f"   Severity : {event['severity']}")
299:         print(f"   CVE hint : {event['cve_hints'][0]}")
300:         print(f"   Payload  : {event['payload_snip'][:80]}")
301: 
302:     engine = AutoShieldEngine(event_callback=on_attack)
303: 
304:     print("=== AutoShield Engine Self-Test ===\n")
305:     for atype in ["SQLi", "XSS", "LFI", "CMDi"]:
306:         engine.simulate_attack(atype, src_ip=f"10.0.0.{['SQLi','XSS','LFI','CMDi'].index(atype)+1}")
307:         time.sleep(0.2)
308: 
309:     print(f"\nTotal events logged: {len(engine.get_log())}")

1: """
2: AutoShield - Auto-Block Module
3: Fires iptables rules to block attacker IPs automatically.
4: Falls back to in-process blocklist when not root (dev mode).
5: """
6: 
7: import subprocess
8: import logging
9: import threading
10: import json
11: import time
12: import os
13: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
14: from collections import defaultdict
15: 
16: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.Blocker")
17: 
18: # ─── Config ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
19: 
20: BLOCK_DURATION_SECONDS = 3600       # 1 hour auto-expiry
21: RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW      = 60         # seconds
22: RATE_LIMIT_THRESHOLD   = 5          # attacks before rate-ban
23: WHITELIST_IPS          = {"127.0.0.1", "::1"}   # never block these
24: 
25: 
26: # ─── iptables helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
27: 
28: def _is_root() -> bool:
29:     return os.geteuid() == 0 if hasattr(os, "geteuid") else False
30: 
31: 
32: def _iptables(action: str, ip: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:
33:     """
34:     action: 'block' | 'unblock'
35:     Returns (success, message)
36:     """
37:     flag = "-A" if action == "block" else "-D"
38:     cmd  = ["iptables", flag, "INPUT", "-s", ip, "-j", "DROP"]
39:     try:
40:         result = subprocess.run(
41:             cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5
42:         )
43:         if result.returncode == 0:
44:             return True, f"iptables {action} {ip} OK"
45:         else:
46:             return False, f"iptables error: {result.stderr.strip()}"
47:     except FileNotFoundError:
48:         return False, "iptables not found (not Linux or not installed)"
49:     except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
50:         return False, "iptables command timed out"
51:     except Exception as e:
52:         return False, str(e)
53: 
54: 
55: # ─── Block Manager ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
56: 
57: class BlockManager:
58:     """
59:     Tracks blocked IPs, fires iptables rules when root,
60:     else maintains in-memory blocklist for dev/demo mode.
61:     """
62: 
63:     def __init__(self):
64:         self._blocked: dict[str, dict] = {}     # ip → block_record
65:         self._attack_counts: dict[str, list]    = defaultdict(list)  # ip → [timestamps]
66:         self._lock = threading.RLock()
67:         self._root = _is_root()
68: 
69:         if not self._root:
70:             log.warning("Not running as root — iptables disabled. Using in-memory blocklist.")
71: 
72:         # Start expiry cleanup thread
73:         self._expiry_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._expiry_loop, daemon=True)
74:         self._expiry_thread.start()
75: 
76:     # ── public API ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
77: 
78:     def block_ip(self, ip: str, reason: str = "attack detected",
79:                  severity: str = "HIGH", attack_type: str = "Unknown") -> dict:
80:         """Block an IP. Returns block record."""
81:         if ip in WHITELIST_IPS:
82:             return {"status": "SKIPPED", "reason": "IP is whitelisted", "ip": ip}
83: 
84:         with self._lock:
85:             if ip in self._blocked:
86:                 return {"status": "ALREADY_BLOCKED", "ip": ip, **self._blocked[ip]}
87: 
88:             expires_at = datetime.now() + timedelta(seconds=BLOCK_DURATION_SECONDS)
89:             record = {
90:                 "ip":          ip,
91:                 "reason":      reason,
92:                 "attack_type": attack_type,
93:                 "severity":    severity,
94:                 "blocked_at":  datetime.now().isoformat(),
95:                 "expires_at":  expires_at.isoformat(),
96:                 "method":      "iptables" if self._root else "in-memory",
97:                 "status":      "BLOCKED",
98:             }
99: 
100:             # Fire iptables if root
101:             if self._root:
102:                 ok, msg = _iptables("block", ip)
103:                 if not ok:
104:                     record["status"]  = "BLOCK_FAILED"
105:                     record["error"]   = msg
106:                     log.error(f"Failed to block {ip}: {msg}")
107:                     return record
108:                 record["iptables_msg"] = msg
109: 
110:             self._blocked[ip] = record
111:             log.warning(
112:                 f"🚫 BLOCKED {ip} | {attack_type} [{severity}] "
113:                 f"| expires {expires_at.strftime('%H:%M:%S')} "
114:                 f"| method={record['method']}"
115:             )
116:             return record
117: 
118:     def unblock_ip(self, ip: str) -> dict:
119:         with self._lock:
120:             if ip not in self._blocked:
121:                 return {"status": "NOT_BLOCKED", "ip": ip}
122: 
123:             record = self._blocked.pop(ip)
124: 
125:             if self._root:
126:                 ok, msg = _iptables("unblock", ip)
127:                 if not ok:
128:                     log.error(f"Failed to unblock {ip}: {msg}")
129: 
130:             log.info(f"✅ UNBLOCKED {ip}")
131:             return {"status": "UNBLOCKED", "ip": ip, "was": record}
132: 
133:     def is_blocked(self, ip: str) -> bool:
134:         with self._lock:
135:             return ip in self._blocked
136: 
137:     def get_blocked_list(self) -> list[dict]:
138:         with self._lock:
139:             return list(self._blocked.values())
140: 
141:     def record_attack(self, ip: str) -> bool:
142:         """
143:         Track attack rate per IP.
144:         Returns True if rate-limit threshold exceeded → caller should block.
145:         """
146:         now = time.time()
147:         with self._lock:
148:             # Prune old timestamps
149:             self._attack_counts[ip] = [
150:                 t for t in self._attack_counts[ip]
151:                 if now - t < RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW
152:             ]
153:             self._attack_counts[ip].append(now)
154:             count = len(self._attack_counts[ip])
155: 
156:         if count >= RATE_LIMIT_THRESHOLD:
157:             log.warning(f"Rate limit hit for {ip}: {count} attacks in {RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW}s")
158:             return True
159:         return False
160: 
161:     def auto_respond(self, event: dict) -> dict:
162:         """
163:         Full auto-defense pipeline for an attack event.
164:         Returns enriched event with action taken.
165:         """
166:         ip          = event.get("src_ip", "0.0.0.0")
167:         attack_type = event.get("attack_type", "Unknown")
168:         severity    = event.get("severity", "HIGH")
169: 
170:         # Always block CRITICAL; rate-limit for others
171:         should_block = (
172:             severity == "CRITICAL"
173:             or self.record_attack(ip)
174:         )
175: 
176:         if should_block:
177:             record = self.block_ip(
178:                 ip,
179:                 reason=f"Auto-blocked: {attack_type}",
180:                 severity=severity,
181:                 attack_type=attack_type,
182:             )
183:             event["action"]   = "BLOCKED"
184:             event["status"]   = "MITIGATED"
185:             event["block_record"] = record
186:         else:
187:             event["action"] = "RATE_MONITORED"
188:             event["status"] = "MONITORING"
189: 
190:         # Input sanitization note (applied at WAF layer in real deploy)
191:         event["sanitization"] = _sanitize_note(attack_type)
192: 
193:         return event
194: 
195:     # ── expiry loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
196: 
197:     def _expiry_loop(self):
198:         while True:
199:             time.sleep(30)
200:             now = datetime.now()
201:             with self._lock:
202:                 expired = [
203:                     ip for ip, rec in self._blocked.items()
204:                     if datetime.fromisoformat(rec["expires_at"]) <= now
205:                 ]
206:             for ip in expired:
207:                 log.info(f"Auto-expiring block for {ip}")
208:                 self.unblock_ip(ip)
209: 
210:     def flush_all(self):
211:         """Emergency: unblock all IPs."""
212:         ips = list(self._blocked.keys())
213:         for ip in ips:
214:             self.unblock_ip(ip)
215:         log.info(f"Flushed {len(ips)} blocked IPs.")
216: 
217:     def stats(self) -> dict:
218:         with self._lock:
219:             return {
220:                 "total_blocked":  len(self._blocked),
221:                 "attack_counters": {
222:                     ip: len(ts) for ip, ts in self._attack_counts.items()
223:                 },
224:                 "root_mode": self._root,
225:             }
226: 
227: 
228: # ─── Input Sanitization Advice ────────────────────────────────────────────────
229: 
230: def _sanitize_note(attack_type: str) -> str:
231:     NOTES = {
232:         "SQLi": "Parameterized queries applied. Input stripped of SQL metacharacters.",
233:         "XSS":  "HTML-encoded output. Script tags neutralized.",
234:         "LFI":  "Path traversal stripped. File access restricted to allowed dir.",
235:         "CMDi": "Shell metacharacters removed. Command execution sandboxed.",
236:     }
237:     return NOTES.get(attack_type, "Input sanitized.")
238: 
239: 
240: # ─── Singleton ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
241: 
242: _blocker_instance: BlockManager | None = None
243: 
244: def get_blocker() -> BlockManager:
245:     global _blocker_instance
246:     if _blocker_instance is None:
247:         _blocker_instance = BlockManager()
248:     return _blocker_instance
249: 
250: 
251: # ─── Quick test ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
252: 
253: if __name__ == "__main__":
254:     blocker = BlockManager()
255: 
256:     test_event = {
257:         "src_ip":      "192.168.1.99",
258:         "attack_type": "SQLi",
259:         "severity":    "CRITICAL",
260:     }
261: 
262:     print("=== AutoShield Blocker Self-Test ===\n")
263:     result = blocker.auto_respond(test_event)
264:     print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, default=str))
265: 
266:     print(f"\nBlocked list: {blocker.get_blocked_list()}")
267:     print(f"Stats: {blocker.stats()}")
268: 
269:     time.sleep(1)
270:     print(f"\nUnblocking...")
271:     blocker.unblock_ip("192.168.1.99")
272:     print(f"Blocked list after unblock: {blocker.get_blocked_list()}")

<path>/home/izumi/Desktop/Everything i make/Cyber_Project/cve_lookup.py</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: """
2: AutoShield - CVE Lookup Module
3: Queries NIST NVD free API for real CVE data matching detected attack types.
4: Caches results to avoid hammering the API.
5: """
6: 
7: import requests
8: import json
9: import time
10: import logging
11: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
12: from functools import lru_cache
13: 
14: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.CVE")
15: 
16: NVD_BASE_URL = "https://services.nvd.nist.gov/rest/json/cves/2.0"
17: CACHE_TTL    = 3600     # 1 hour cache
18: REQUEST_DELAY = 0.6     # NVD rate limit: ~100 req/min without API key
19: 
20: 
21: # ─── Search Keywords per Attack Type ─────────────────────────────────────────
22: 
23: ATTACK_KEYWORDS = {
24:     "SQLi": "SQL injection",
25:     "XSS":  "cross-site scripting",
26:     "LFI":  "local file inclusion path traversal",
27:     "CMDi": "command injection OS injection",
28: }
29: 
30: # ─── Severity → CVSS score filter ─────────────────────────────────────────────
31: 
32: CVSS_MIN = {
33:     "CRITICAL": 9.0,
34:     "HIGH":     7.0,
35:     "MEDIUM":   4.0,
36:     "LOW":      0.0,
37: }
38: 
39: # ─── In-memory cache ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
40: 
41: _cache: dict[str, tuple[list, float]] = {}   # key → (results, timestamp)
42: 
43: 
44: def _cached(key: str) -> list | None:
45:     if key in _cache:
46:         results, ts = _cache[key]
47:         if time.time() - ts < CACHE_TTL:
48:             return results
49:     return None
50: 
51: 
52: def _store(key: str, results: list):
53:     _cache[key] = (results, time.time())
54: 
55: 
56: # ─── NVD API fetch ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
57: 
58: def fetch_cves(attack_type: str, max_results: int = 5) -> list[dict]:
59:     """
60:     Query NVD for CVEs matching attack_type.
61:     Returns list of CVE summary dicts.
62:     """
63:     cache_key = f"{attack_type}:{max_results}"
64:     cached = _cached(cache_key)
65:     if cached is not None:
66:         log.debug(f"CVE cache hit for {attack_type}")
67:         return cached
68: 
69:     keyword = ATTACK_KEYWORDS.get(attack_type, attack_type)
70: 
71:     params = {
72:         "keywordSearch": keyword,
73:         "resultsPerPage": max_results,
74:         "startIndex": 0,
75:     }
76: 
77:     try:
78:         log.info(f"Querying NVD for: {keyword}")
79:         time.sleep(REQUEST_DELAY)   # respect rate limit
80: 
81:         resp = requests.get(
82:             NVD_BASE_URL,
83:             params=params,
84:             timeout=10,
85:             headers={"User-Agent": "AutoShield/1.0 (security-research)"},
86:         )
87:         resp.raise_for_status()
88:         data = resp.json()
89: 
90:     except requests.exceptions.Timeout:
91:         log.warning("NVD API timeout — using fallback CVEs")
92:         return _fallback_cves(attack_type)
93:     except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError:
94:         log.warning("NVD API unreachable — using fallback CVEs")
95:         return _fallback_cves(attack_type)
96:     except Exception as e:
97:         log.error(f"NVD API error: {e}")
98:         return _fallback_cves(attack_type)
99: 
100:     results = []
101:     for vuln in data.get("vulnerabilities", []):
102:         cve_data = vuln.get("cve", {})
103:         cve_id   = cve_data.get("id", "UNKNOWN")
104: 
105:         # Description (English)
106:         descriptions = cve_data.get("descriptions", [])
107:         desc = next(
108:             (d["value"] for d in descriptions if d.get("lang") == "en"),
109:             "No description available."
110:         )
111: 
112:         # CVSS score
113:         metrics  = cve_data.get("metrics", {})
114:         cvss_v31 = metrics.get("cvssMetricV31", [{}])[0] if metrics.get("cvssMetricV31") else {}
115:         cvss_v30 = metrics.get("cvssMetricV30", [{}])[0] if metrics.get("cvssMetricV30") else {}
116:         cvss_v2  = metrics.get("cvssMetricV2",  [{}])[0] if metrics.get("cvssMetricV2")  else {}
117: 
118:         score_data = cvss_v31 or cvss_v30 or cvss_v2
119:         base_score = score_data.get("cvssData", {}).get("baseScore", "N/A")
120:         severity_label = score_data.get("cvssData", {}).get("baseSeverity", "UNKNOWN")
121: 
122:         # Published date
123:         published = cve_data.get("published", "")[:10]
124: 
125:         # References
126:         refs = cve_data.get("references", [])
127:         top_ref = refs[0].get("url", "") if refs else ""
128: 
129:         results.append({
130:             "cve_id":       cve_id,
131:             "description":  desc[:300] + ("..." if len(desc) > 300 else ""),
132:             "cvss_score":   base_score,
133:             "severity":     severity_label,
134:             "published":    published,
135:             "reference":    top_ref,
136:             "attack_type":  attack_type,
137:         })
138: 
139:     if not results:
140:         results = _fallback_cves(attack_type)
141: 
142:     _store(cache_key, results)
143:     return results
144: 
145: 
146: def fetch_cve_by_id(cve_id: str) -> dict | None:
147:     """Fetch single CVE by ID (e.g. CVE-2023-23752)."""
148:     cache_key = f"id:{cve_id}"
149:     cached = _cached(cache_key)
150:     if cached:
151:         return cached[0] if cached else None
152: 
153:     try:
154:         time.sleep(REQUEST_DELAY)
155:         resp = requests.get(
156:             NVD_BASE_URL,
157:             params={"cveId": cve_id},
158:             timeout=10,
159:             headers={"User-Agent": "AutoShield/1.0"},
160:         )
161:         resp.raise_for_status()
162:         data = resp.json()
163:         vulns = data.get("vulnerabilities", [])
164:         if not vulns:
165:             return None
166: 
167:         cve_data = vulns[0]["cve"]
168:         desc = next(
169:             (d["value"] for d in cve_data.get("descriptions", []) if d.get("lang") == "en"),
170:             "No description."
171:         )
172:         metrics  = cve_data.get("metrics", {})
173:         score_data = (
174:             (metrics.get("cvssMetricV31") or [{}])[0]
175:             or (metrics.get("cvssMetricV30") or [{}])[0]
176:             or {}
177:         )
178:         result = {
179:             "cve_id":      cve_id,
180:             "description": desc[:400],
181:             "cvss_score":  score_data.get("cvssData", {}).get("baseScore", "N/A"),
182:             "severity":    score_data.get("cvssData", {}).get("baseSeverity", "UNKNOWN"),
183:             "published":   cve_data.get("published", "")[:10],
184:         }
185:         _store(cache_key, [result])
186:         return result
187: 
188:     except Exception as e:
189:         log.error(f"CVE ID lookup failed for {cve_id}: {e}")
190:         return None
191: 
192: 
193: # ─── Fallback CVE data (no network needed) ────────────────────────────────────
194: 
195: FALLBACK_CVES = {
196:     "SQLi": [
197:         {"cve_id": "CVE-2023-23752", "description": "Joomla improper access check allows SQL injection via crafted API requests.", "cvss_score": 9.8, "severity": "CRITICAL", "published": "2023-02-16", "attack_type": "SQLi", "reference": "https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2023-23752"},

225:     Tries live NVD first, falls back to static data.

187: 
188: def fire_alert(event: dict, force: bool = False) -> dict:
189:     """
190:     Send all configured alerts for an event.
191:     Only fires for CRITICAL/HIGH. Throttled per IP.
192:     force=True bypasses throttle (for testing).
193:     """
194:     severity = event.get("severity","LOW")
195:     ip       = event.get("src_ip","?")
196:

198:         return {"status": "SKIPPED", "reason": f"Severity {severity} below threshold"}

213: 
214:     log.info(f"Alert fired for {ip}: {results}")

216:

<content>
1: """
2: AutoShield - Attack Map
3: Geolocates attacker IPs and renders a live threat map using Folium.
4: Uses ip-api.com free tier (no key needed, 45 req/min).
5: """
6: 
7: import requests
8: import folium
9: import json
10: import time
11: import logging
12: import os
13: from datetime import datetime
14: from collections import defaultdict
15: 
16: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.AttackMap")
17: 
18: IP_API_URL  = "http://ip-api.com/json/{ip}?fields=status,country,regionName,city,lat,lon,isp,org,query"
19: CACHE_FILE  = "/tmp/autoshield_geo_cache.json"
20: RATE_LIMIT  = 0.8   # seconds between requests (45/min safe limit)
21: 
22: # ─── Geo cache (persist between runs) ────────────────────────────────────────
23: 
24: def _load_cache() -> dict:
25:     try:
26:         with open(CACHE_FILE) as f:
27:             return json.load(f)
28:     except Exception:
29:         return {}
30: 
31: def _save_cache(cache: dict):
32:     try:
33:         with open(CACHE_FILE, "w") as f:
34:             json.dump(cache, f)
35:     except Exception:
36:         pass
37: 
38: _geo_cache = _load_cache()
39: 
40: # Known private/local IP ranges → skip API call
41: _PRIVATE_PREFIXES = ("10.", "192.168.", "172.16.", "172.17.", "127.", "::1", "0.0.0.0")
42: 
43: def _is_private(ip: str) -> bool:
44:     return any(ip.startswith(p) for p in _PRIVATE_PREFIXES)
45: 
46: # Fake geo for private IPs (demo mode: place them near India)
47: _DEMO_LOCATIONS = [
48:     {"country": "India",        "city": "New Delhi",  "lat": 28.6139, "lon": 77.2090, "isp": "Demo ISP"},
49:     {"country": "China",        "city": "Beijing",    "lat": 39.9042, "lon": 116.4074,"isp": "China Telecom"},
50:     {"country": "Russia",       "city": "Moscow",     "lat": 55.7558, "lon": 37.6173, "isp": "Rostelecom"},
51:     {"country": "United States","city": "Ashburn",    "lat": 39.0438, "lon": -77.4874,"isp": "Amazon AWS"},
52:     {"country": "Germany",      "city": "Frankfurt",  "lat": 50.1109, "lon": 8.6821,  "isp": "Hetzner"},
53:     {"country": "Brazil",       "city": "São Paulo",  "lat": -23.5505,"lon": -46.6333,"isp": "Claro"},
54:     {"country": "India",        "city": "Mumbai",     "lat": 19.0760, "lon": 72.8777, "isp": "Reliance Jio"},
55:     {"country": "Netherlands",  "city": "Amsterdam",  "lat": 52.3676, "lon": 4.9041,  "isp": "Digital Ocean"},
56: ]
57: 
58: _demo_idx = 0
59: 
60: def geolocate_ip(ip: str) -> dict:
61:     """Return geo dict for an IP. Cached, rate-limited."""
62:     global _demo_idx
63: 
64:     if ip in _geo_cache:
65:         return _geo_cache[ip]
66: 
67:     if _is_private(ip):
68:         # Rotate through demo locations for private IPs
69:         loc = dict(_DEMO_LOCATIONS[_demo_idx % len(_DEMO_LOCATIONS)])
70:         loc["query"] = ip
71:         loc["status"] = "demo"
72:         _demo_idx += 1
73:         _geo_cache[ip] = loc
74:         _save_cache(_geo_cache)
75:         return loc
76: 
77:     try:
78:         time.sleep(RATE_LIMIT)
79:         resp = requests.get(IP_API_URL.format(ip=ip), timeout=5)
80:         data = resp.json()
81:         if data.get("status") == "success":
82:             _geo_cache[ip] = data
83:             _save_cache(_geo_cache)
84:             return data
85:     except Exception as e:
86:         log.error(f"Geo lookup failed for {ip}: {e}")
87: 
88:     # Fallback
89:     fallback = {"country": "Unknown", "city": "Unknown", "lat": 20.5937, "lon": 78.9629,
90:                 "isp": "Unknown", "query": ip, "status": "fallback"}
91:     return fallback
92: 
93: 
94: # ─── Map builder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
95: 
96: SEVERITY_COLORS = {
97:     "CRITICAL": "#ef4444",
98:     "HIGH":     "#f97316",
99:     "MEDIUM":   "#eab308",
100:     "LOW":      "#22c55e",
101: }
102: 
103: ATTACK_ICONS = {
104:     "SQLi": "💉",
105:     "XSS":  "📝",
106:     "LFI":  "📂",
107:     "CMDi": "💻",
108: }
109: 
110: def build_attack_map(attack_events: list[dict], output_path: str = "/tmp/autoshield_map.html") -> str:
111:     """
112:     Build Folium map from attack events list.
113:     Returns path to generated HTML file.
114:     """
115:     # Center on India
116:     m = folium.Map(
117:         location=[20.5937, 78.9629],
118:         zoom_start=3,
119:         tiles="CartoDB dark_matter",
120:     )
121: 
122:     # Aggregate attacks per IP
123:     ip_attacks: dict[str, list] = defaultdict(list)
124:     for event in attack_events:
125:         ip_attacks[event.get("src_ip", "0.0.0.0")].append(event)
126: 
127:     for ip, events in ip_attacks.items():
128:         geo   = geolocate_ip(ip)
129:         lat   = geo.get("lat", 20.5937)
130:         lon   = geo.get("lon", 78.9629)
131:         count = len(events)
132: 
133:         # Use worst severity for color
134:         sev_order = ["CRITICAL", "HIGH", "MEDIUM", "LOW"]
135:         severities = [e.get("severity","LOW") for e in events]
136:         worst_sev  = next((s for s in sev_order if s in severities), "LOW")
137:         color      = SEVERITY_COLORS.get(worst_sev, "#ef4444")
138: 
139:         # Attack type summary
140:         types = list({e.get("attack_type","?") for e in events})
141:         icons = " ".join(ATTACK_ICONS.get(t,"⚠️") for t in types)
142: 
143:         # Popup HTML
144:         latest  = events[-1]
145:         popup_html = f"""
146:         <div style="font-family:monospace;background:#1e1e1e;color:#e6edf3;
147:                     padding:12px;border-radius:6px;min-width:220px">
148:           <b style="color:{color}">⚠ {worst_sev} ATTACK</b><br/>
149:           <hr style="border-color:#444;margin:6px 0"/>
150:           <b>IP:</b> {ip}<br/>
151:           <b>Location:</b> {geo.get('city','?')}, {geo.get('country','?')}<br/>
152:           <b>ISP:</b> {geo.get('isp','?')[:30]}<br/>
153:           <b>Attacks:</b> {count} ({', '.join(types)})<br/>
154:           <b>Status:</b> <span style="color:#22c55e">{latest.get('action','DETECTED')}</span><br/>
155:           <b>Last:</b> {latest.get('timestamp','')[-8:-3]}<br/>
156:           <b>CVE:</b> {latest.get('cve_hints',['?'])[0]}
157:         </div>
158:         """
159: 
160:         # Pulse circle for severity
161:         radius = min(8 + count * 3, 25)
162:         folium.CircleMarker(
163:             location=[lat, lon],
164:             radius=radius,
165:             color=color,
166:             fill=True,
167:             fill_color=color,
168:             fill_opacity=0.7,
169:             popup=folium.Popup(popup_html, max_width=280),
170:             tooltip=f"{icons} {ip} ({count} attacks)",
171:         ).add_to(m)
172: 
173:         # Arrow line to Indian server (demo: target = New Delhi)
174:         if geo.get("country") != "India" or geo.get("status") != "demo":
175:             folium.PolyLine(
176:                 locations=[[lat, lon], [28.6139, 77.2090]],
177:                 color=color,
178:                 weight=1.5,
179:                 opacity=0.4,
180:                 dash_array="5 5",
181:             ).add_to(m)
182: 
183:     # Target server marker
184:     folium.Marker(
185:         location=[28.6139, 77.2090],
186:         popup="🛡️ AutoShield Protected Server",
187:         icon=folium.Icon(color="green", icon="shield", prefix="fa"),
188:         tooltip="🛡️ Protected Server",
189:     ).add_to(m)
190: 
191:     # Legend
192:     legend_html = """
193:     <div style="position:fixed;bottom:30px;left:30px;background:#1e1e1e;
194:                 border:1px solid #444;padding:12px;border-radius:8px;
195:                 font-family:monospace;color:#e6edf3;font-size:12px;z-index:9999">
196:       <b>🛡️ AutoShield Threat Map</b><br/><br/>
197:       <span style="color:#ef4444">●</span> CRITICAL &nbsp;
198:       <span style="color:#f97316">●</span> HIGH<br/>
199:       <span style="color:#eab308">●</span> MEDIUM &nbsp;
200:       <span style="color:#22c55e">●</span> LOW<br/><br/>
201:       💉 SQLi &nbsp; 📝 XSS<br/>
202:       📂 LFI &nbsp; 💻 CMDi
203:     </div>
204:     """
205:     m.get_root().html.add_child(folium.Element(legend_html))
206: 
207:     m.save(output_path)
208:     log.info(f"Attack map saved: {output_path}")
209:     return output_path
210: 
211: 
212: def get_geo_stats(attack_events: list[dict]) -> dict:
213:     """Summary geo stats for dashboard."""
214:     countries = defaultdict(int)
215:     for event in attack_events:
216:         ip  = event.get("src_ip","0.0.0.0")
217:         geo = geolocate_ip(ip)
218:         countries[geo.get("country","Unknown")] += 1
219: 
220:     return {
221:         "top_countries": sorted(countries.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5],
222:         "unique_ips":    len({e.get("src_ip") for e in attack_events}),
223:         "total_attacks": len(attack_events),
224:     }
225: 
226: 
227: # ─── Self-test ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
228: 
229: if __name__ == "__main__":
230:     print("=== Attack Map Self-Test ===\n")
231:

234:          "action": "BLOCKED", "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
235:          "cve_hints": ["CVE-2023-23752"]},
236:         {"src_ip": "192.168.1.2",  "attack_type": "XSS",  "severity": "HIGH",
237:          "action": "BLOCKED", "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
238:          "cve_hints": ["CVE-2023-32315"]},
239:         {"src_ip": "192.168.1.3",  "attack_type": "LFI",  "severity": "CRITICAL",

<content>
1: """
2: AutoShield - Threat Score Engine
3: Computes 0-100 threat score per IP using feature engineering + ML heuristics.
4: No training data needed — rule-based scoring with ML-style feature weighting.
5: """
6: 
7: import math
8: import time
9: import logging
10: from collections import defaultdict
11: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
12: 
13: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.ThreatScore")
14: 
15: # ─── Feature weights (simulate trained model coefficients) ────────────────────
16: 
17: WEIGHTS = {
18:     "attack_count":         0.25,   # raw volume
19:     "attack_diversity":     0.20,   # how many different attack types
20:     "severity_score":       0.20,   # weighted severity
21:     "time_density":         0.15,   # attacks per minute
22:     "repeat_offender":      0.10,   # seen in previous sessions
23:     "payload_sophistication": 0.10, # match count per attack
24: }
25: 
26: SEVERITY_WEIGHTS = {
27:     "CRITICAL": 10,
28:     "HIGH":     7,
29:     "MEDIUM":   4,
30:     "LOW":      1,
31: }
32: 
33: ATTACK_TYPE_RISK = {
34:     "CMDi": 1.0,
35:     "SQLi": 0.95,
36:     "LFI":  0.90,
37:     "XSS":  0.70,
38: }
39: 
40: # ─── Per-IP state ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
41: 
42: class IPProfile:
43:     def __init__(self, ip: str):
44:         self.ip              = ip
45:         self.events: list    = []
46:         self.first_seen      = datetime.now()
47:         self.last_seen       = datetime.now()
48:         self.threat_score    = 0
49:         self.threat_label    = "CLEAN"
50:         self.seen_previously = False
51: 
52:     def add_event(self, event: dict):
53:         self.events.append(event)
54:         self.last_seen = datetime.now()
55: 
56:     def to_dict(self) -> dict:
57:         return {
58:             "ip":           self.ip,
59:             "threat_score": self.threat_score,
60:             "threat_label": self.threat_label,
61:             "attack_count": len(self.events),
62:             "attack_types": list({e.get("attack_type","?") for e in self.events}),
63:             "first_seen":   self.first_seen.isoformat(),
64:             "last_seen":    self.last_seen.isoformat(),
65:             "worst_severity": self._worst_severity(),
66:         }
67: 
68:     def _worst_severity(self) -> str:
69:         for sev in ["CRITICAL","HIGH","MEDIUM","LOW"]:
70:             if any(e.get("severity") == sev for e in self.events):
71:                 return sev
72:         return "UNKNOWN"
73: 
74: 
75: # ─── Threat Score Engine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
76: 
77: class ThreatScoreEngine:
78:     def __init__(self):
79:         self._profiles: dict[str, IPProfile] = {}
80:         self._global_ip_history: set          = set()   # IPs seen across sessions
81: 
82:     def ingest(self, event: dict) -> dict:
83:         """
84:         Process new attack event → update IP profile → recalculate score.
85:         Returns updated profile dict.
86:         """
87:         ip = event.get("src_ip", "0.0.0.0")
88:         if ip not in self._profiles:
89:             self._profiles[ip] = IPProfile(ip)
90:         profile = self._profiles[ip]
91: 
92:         # Mark repeat offender if seen before
93:         if ip in self._global_ip_history:
94:             profile.seen_previously = True
95:         self._global_ip_history.add(ip)
96: 
97:         profile.add_event(event)
98:         profile.threat_score = self._calculate_score(profile)
99:         profile.threat_label = self._label(profile.threat_score)
100: 
101:         return profile.to_dict()
102: 
103:     def _calculate_score(self, profile: IPProfile) -> int:
104:         """
105:         Feature engineering → weighted score → sigmoid normalize to 0-100.
106:         """
107:         events = profile.events
108:         n      = len(events)
109:         if n == 0:
110:             return 0
111: 
112:         # F1: Attack count (log scale, saturates at ~20 attacks)
113:         f_count = min(math.log1p(n) / math.log1p(20), 1.0)
114: 
115:         # F2: Attack diversity (how many different types, max 4)
116:         types   = {e.get("attack_type","?") for e in events}
117:         f_div   = len(types) / 4.0
118: 
119:         # F3: Severity score (weighted average normalized to 0-1)
120:         sev_total = sum(
121:             SEVERITY_WEIGHTS.get(e.get("severity","LOW"), 1)
122:             for e in events
123:         )
124:         sev_max = SEVERITY_WEIGHTS["CRITICAL"] * n
125:         f_sev   = min(sev_total / max(sev_max, 1), 1.0)
126: 
127:         # F4: Time density — attacks per minute in the last 5 minutes
128:         now  = datetime.now()
129:         window_start = now - timedelta(minutes=5)
130:         recent = [
131:             e for e in events
132:             if datetime.fromisoformat(e.get("timestamp", now.isoformat())) > window_start
133:         ]
134:         density = len(recent) / 5.0   # attacks per minute
135:         f_density = min(density / 3.0, 1.0)   # saturates at 3 attacks/min
136: 
137:         # F5: Repeat offender
138:         f_repeat = 1.0 if profile.seen_previously else 0.0
139: 
140:         # F6: Payload sophistication (avg match count per event)
141:         match_counts = [len(e.get("matched_rules", [])) for e in events]
142:         avg_matches  = sum(match_counts) / max(len(match_counts), 1)
143:         f_sophist    = min(avg_matches / 5.0, 1.0)
144: 
145:         # F7: Attack type risk multiplier
146:         type_risks = [ATTACK_TYPE_RISK.get(e.get("attack_type","XSS"), 0.5) for e in events]
147:         f_type_risk = sum(type_risks) / max(len(type_risks), 1)
148: 
149:         # Weighted sum
150:         raw_score = (
151:             WEIGHTS["attack_count"]          * f_count    +
152:             WEIGHTS["attack_diversity"]      * f_div      +
153:             WEIGHTS["severity_score"]        * f_sev      +
154:             WEIGHTS["time_density"]          * f_density  +
155:             WEIGHTS["repeat_offender"]       * f_repeat   +
156:             WEIGHTS["payload_sophistication"]* f_sophist
157:         )
158: 
159:         # Apply type risk multiplier
160:         raw_score = raw_score * (0.5 + 0.5 * f_type_risk)
161: 
162:         # Sigmoid-ish normalization to 0-100
163:         score = int(raw_score * 100)
164:         return min(score, 100)
165: 
166:     @staticmethod
167:     def _label(score: int) -> str:
168:         if score >= 80: return "CRITICAL THREAT"
169:         if score >= 60: return "HIGH THREAT"
170:         if score >= 40: return "MEDIUM THREAT"
171:         if score >= 20: return "LOW THREAT"
172:         return "CLEAN"
173: 
174:     def get_profile(self, ip: str) -> dict | None:
175:         if ip not in self._profiles:
176:             return None
177:         return self._profiles[ip].to_dict()
178: 
179:     def get_all_profiles(self, min_score: int = 0) -> list[dict]:
180:         profiles = [
181:             p.to_dict() for p in self._profiles.values()
182:             if p.threat_score >= min_score
183:         ]
184:         return sorted(profiles, key=lambda x: x["threat_score"], reverse=True)
185: 
186:     def get_top_threats(self, n: int = 5) -> list[dict]:
187:         return self.get_all_profiles()[:n]
188: 
189:     def score_bar(self, score: int, width: int = 20) -> str:
190:         """ASCII bar for terminal display."""
191:         filled = int(score / 100 * width)
192:         bar    = "█" * filled + "░" * (width - filled)
193:         color_prefix = ""
194:         if score >= 80:   color_prefix = "\033[91m"
195:         elif score >= 60: color_prefix = "\033[93m"
196:         elif score >= 40: color_prefix = "\033[94m"
197:         return f"{color_prefix}[{bar}]\033[0m {score:3d}/100"
198: 
199: 
200: # ─── Singleton ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
201: 
202: _engine: ThreatScoreEngine | None = None
203: 
204: def get_threat_engine() -> ThreatScoreEngine:
205:     global _engine
206:     if _engine is None:
207:         _engine = ThreatScoreEngine()
208:     return _engine
209: 
210: 
211: # ─── Self-test ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
212: 
213: if __name__ == "__main__":
214:     from datetime import datetime
215: 
216:     engine = ThreatScoreEngine()
217:     print("=== Threat Score Engine Self-Test ===\n")
218: 
219:     TEST_SEQUENCES = [
220:         # Persistent SQLi attacker
221:         [("10.0.0.1", "SQLi",  "CRITICAL", 3),
222:          ("10.0.0.1", "SQLi",  "CRITICAL", 3),
223:          ("10.0.0.1", "LFI",   "CRITICAL", 2),
224:          ("10.0.0.1", "CMDi",  "CRITICAL", 3)],
225:         # Single XSS probe
226:         [("10.0.0.2", "XSS",   "HIGH",     2)],
227:         # Mixed low-confidence
228:         [("10.0.0.3", "SQLi",  "HIGH",     1),
229:          ("10.0.0.3", "XSS",   "MEDIUM",   1)],
230:         # Aggressive multi-vector
231:         [("10.0.0.4", "CMDi",  "CRITICAL", 5),
232:          ("10.0.0.4", "SQLi",  "CRITICAL", 4),
233:          ("10.0.0.4", "LFI",   "CRITICAL", 3),
234:          ("10.0.0.4", "XSS",   "HIGH",     2),
235:          ("10.0.0.4", "CMDi",  "CRITICAL", 4)],
236:     ]
237: 
238:     for seq in TEST_SEQUENCES:
239:         for ip, atype, severity, matches in seq:
240:             event = {
241:                 "src_ip":       ip,
242:                 "attack_type":  atype,
243:                 "severity":     severity,
244:                 "matched_rules": ["rule"] * matches,
245:                 "timestamp":    datetime.now().isoformat(),
246:             }
247:             profile = engine.ingest(event)
248: 
249:     print("Top threats:")
250:     for p in engine.get_top_threats(5):
251:         bar   = engine.score_bar(p["threat_score"])
252:         label = p["threat_label"]
253:         print(f"  {p['ip']:<14} {bar}  {label:<20} types={p['attack_types']}")
254: 
255:     print()
256:     print(f"Total IPs tracked: {len(engine.get_all_profiles())}")

(End of file - total 256 lines)

<content>
1: """
2: AutoShield - PDF Incident Report Generator
3: One-click compliance report using ReportLab (free).
4: Generates professional PDF: executive summary + attack table + CVE cards + recommendations.
5: """
6: 
7: import os
8: import json
9: import logging
10: from datetime import datetime
11: from collections import defaultdict, Counter
12: 
13: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.Report")
14: 
15: try:
16:     from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import A4
17:     from reportlab.lib.styles   import getSampleStyleSheet, ParagraphStyle
18:     from reportlab.lib.units    import cm
19:     from reportlab.lib           import colors
20:     from reportlab.platypus      import (
21:         SimpleDocTemplate, Paragraph, Spacer, Table, TableStyle,
22:         HRFlowable, PageBreak, KeepTogether,
23:     )
24:     from reportlab.lib.enums    import TA_CENTER, TA_LEFT, TA_RIGHT
25:     REPORTLAB_OK = True
26: except ImportError:
27:     REPORTLAB_OK = False
28:     log.warning("reportlab not installed. Run: pip install reportlab")
29: 
30: 
31: # ─── Color palette ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
32: 
33: C_BG       = colors.HexColor("#0d1117")
34: C_SURFACE  = colors.HexColor("#161b22")
35: C_BORDER   = colors.HexColor("#30363d")
36: C_RED      = colors.HexColor("#ef4444")
37: C_ORANGE   = colors.HexColor("#f97316")
38: C_YELLOW   = colors.HexColor("#eab308")
39: C_GREEN    = colors.HexColor("#22c55e")

44:

46:     "CRITICAL": C_RED,

81:     def style(name, **kwargs):
82:         return ParagraphStyle(name, parent=styles["Normal"], **kwargs)
83: 
84:     S_TITLE     = style("title",    fontSize=24, textColor=C_WHITE,
85:                          fontName="Helvetica-Bold", spaceAfter=4,
86:                          alignment=TA_CENTER)

88:                          alignment=TA_CENTER, spaceAfter=20)
89:     S_H1        = style("h1",       fontSize=14, textColor=C_WHITE,
90:                          fontName="Helvetica-Bold", spaceBefore=16, spaceAfter=8)
91:     S_H2        = style("h2",       fontSize=11, textColor=C_BLUE,
92:                          fontName="Helvetica-Bold", spaceBefore=10, spaceAfter=6)
93:     S_BODY      = style("body",     fontSize=9,  textColor=C_TEXT,
94:                          leading=14, spaceAfter=6)
95:     S_MUTED     = style("muted",    fontSize=8,  textColor=C_MUTED,

<content>
1: """
2: AutoShield - CERT-In Feed Integration
3: Pulls India-specific advisories from CERT-In + NVD, cross-references with live attacks.
4: CERT-In public: https://www.cert-in.org.in/s2cMainServlet?pageid=PUBVLNOTES01
5: NVD feed filtered for Indian software/infra CVEs.
6: """
7: 
8: import requests
9: import json
10: import time
11: import logging
12: import re
13: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
14: from xml.etree import ElementTree as ET
15: 
16: log = logging.getLogger("AutoShield.CERTIn")
17: 
18: # ─── CERT-In public RSS/XML feed ──────────────────────────────────────────────
19: 
20: CERTIN_RSS     = "https://www.cert-in.org.in/RSS.jsp"
21: NVD_BASE       = "https://services.nvd.nist.gov/rest/json/cves/2.0"
22: CACHE_TTL      = 1800   # 30 min
23: 
24: _cache: dict = {}
25: 
26: # ─── Indian software / vendor keywords ───────────────────────────────────────
27: 
28: INDIA_KEYWORDS = [
29:     # Govt portals & stacks
30:     "IRCTC", "Aadhaar", "DigiLocker", "NPCI", "UPI", "BHIM",
31:     "NIC", "eMitra", "eGov", "mSeva", "e-district",
32:     # Indian ISVs & unicorns
33:     "Zoho", "Freshworks", "Tata", "Infosys", "Wipro", "HCL",
34:     "Juspay", "Razorpay", "PhonePe", "Paytm", "Zerodha",
35:     # Common Indian hosting & infra
36:     "BSNL", "MTNL", "Airtel", "Jio", "NIC Cloud",
37:     # Generic high-impact (CERT-In issues advisories for these)
38:     "Apache", "WordPress", "OpenSSL", "Log4j",
39: ]
40: 
41: # CERT-In severity mapping
42: CERTIN_SEVERITY = {
43:     "Critical": "CRITICAL",
44:     "High":     "HIGH",
45:     "Medium":   "MEDIUM",
46:     "Low":      "LOW",
47: }
48: 
49: 
50: # ─── Fetch CERT-In RSS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
51: 
52: def fetch_certin_advisories(max_items: int = 10) -> list[dict]:
53:     """
54:     Pull latest advisories from CERT-In RSS feed.
55:     Falls back to NVD India-relevant search if RSS unreachable.
56:     """
57:     cache_key = f"certin:{max_items}"
58:     if cache_key in _cache:
59:         data, ts = _cache[cache_key]
60:         if time.time() - ts < CACHE_TTL:
61:             return data
62: 
63:     try:
64:         log.info("Fetching CERT-In RSS feed...")
65:         resp = requests.get(CERTIN_RSS, timeout=8,
66:                             headers={"User-Agent": "AutoShield/1.0"})
67:         resp.raise_for_status()
68:         items = _parse_certin_rss(resp.text, max_items)
69:         if items:
70:             _cache[cache_key] = (items, time.time())
71:             return items
72:     except Exception as e:
73:         log.warning(f"CERT-In RSS failed: {e} — falling back to NVD India search")
74: 
75:     # Fallback: NVD search for Indian-relevant CVEs
76:     items = _fetch_nvd_india_cves(max_items)
77:     _cache[cache_key] = (items, time.time())
78:     return items
79: 
80: 
81: def _parse_certin_rss(xml_text: str, max_items: int) -> list[dict]:
82:     """Parse CERT-In RSS XML into advisory dicts."""
83:     try:
84:         root  = ET.fromstring(xml_text)
85:         items = []
86:         for item in root.findall(".//item")[:max_items]:
87:             title = item.findtext("title", "").strip()
88:             link  = item.findtext("link",  "").strip()
89:             desc  = item.findtext("description", "").strip()
90:             pub   = item.findtext("pubDate", "")[:16]
91: 
92:             # Extract advisory ID + severity from title
93:             adv_id   = re.search(r"CIVN-\d{4}-\d+", title)
94:             severity = next(
95:                 (CERTIN_SEVERITY[s] for s in CERTIN_SEVERITY if s.lower() in title.lower()),
96:                 "HIGH"
97:             )
98: 
99:             items.append({
100:                 "source":      "CERT-In",
101:                 "advisory_id": adv_id.group() if adv_id else title[:20],
102:                 "title":       title,
103:                 "description": desc[:300],
104:                 "severity":    severity,
105:                 "published":   pub,
106:                 "link":        link,
107:                 "india_relevant": True,
108:             })
109:         return items
110:     except ET.ParseError as e:
111:         log.error(f"CERT-In XML parse error: {e}")
112:         return []
113: 
114: 
115: def _fetch_nvd_india_cves(max_items: int) -> list[dict]:
116:     """Search NVD for CVEs matching Indian software keywords."""
117:     results = []
118:     # Rotate through a few keywords to get variety
119:     for keyword in ["Zoho", "IRCTC", "Apache", "WordPress"][:2]:
120:         try:
121:             time.sleep(0.6)
122:             resp = requests.get(
123:                 NVD_BASE,
124:                 params={"keywordSearch": keyword, "resultsPerPage": 3},
125:                 timeout=8,
126:                 headers={"User-Agent": "AutoShield/1.0"},
127:             )
128:             resp.raise_for_status()
129:             data = resp.json()
130:             for v in data.get("vulnerabilities", []):
131:                 cve = v["cve"]
132:                 desc = next(
133:                     (d["value"] for d in cve.get("descriptions", []) if d.get("lang") == "en"),
134:                     ""
135:                 )
136:                 metrics    = cve.get("metrics", {})
137:                 score_data = (
138:                     (metrics.get("cvssMetricV31") or [{}])[0].get("cvssData", {})
139:                 )
140:                 results.append({
141:                     "source":      "NVD (India-relevant)",
142:                     "advisory_id": cve.get("id",""),
143:                     "title":       f"{cve.get('id','')} — {keyword}",
144:                     "description": desc[:300],
145:                     "severity":    score_data.get("baseSeverity","HIGH"),
146:                     "cvss_score":  score_data.get("baseScore","N/A"),
147:                     "published":   cve.get("published","")[:10],
148:                     "link":        f"https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/{cve.get('id','')}",
149:                     "india_relevant": True,
150:                     "keyword":     keyword,
151:                 })
152:         except Exception as e:
153:             log.error(f"NVD fetch error for {keyword}: {e}")
154: 
155:     # Merge with static fallback to always have data
156:     if not results:
157:         results = STATIC_CERTIN_ADVISORIES
158: 
159:     _cache[f"certin:{max_items}"] = (results[:max_items], time.time())
160:     return results[:max_items]
161: 
162: 
163: def match_attack_to_certin(attack_type: str, payload: str = "") -> list[dict]:
164:     """
165:     Given a live detected attack, find matching CERT-In advisories.
166:     Returns top 3 relevant advisories.
167:     """
168:     advisories = fetch_certin_advisories(max_items=20)
169:     ATTACK_CERTIN_KEYWORDS = {
170:         "SQLi": ["sql", "injection", "database", "mysql", "postgresql"],
171:         "XSS":  ["xss", "cross-site", "scripting", "javascript", "html"],
172:         "LFI":  ["file", "inclusion", "path", "traversal", "local"],
173:         "CMDi": ["command", "injection", "rce", "remote", "execution", "shell"],
174:     }
175:     keywords = ATTACK_CERTIN_KEYWORDS.get(attack_type, [])
176:     matches  = []
177:     for adv in advisories:
178:         text = (adv.get("title","") + " " + adv.get("description","")).lower()
179:         if any(k in text for k in keywords):
180:             matches.append(adv)
181:     return matches[:3] if matches else advisories[:2]

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 7.2s)

Run it end-to-end like this:

- From project folder: `cd "/home/izumi/Desktop/Everything i make/Cyber_Project"`
- Install deps (if not already): `pip install -r requirements.txt`
- Start dashboard: `streamlit run dashboard.py`
- Open local URL Streamlit prints (usually `http://localhost:8501`)

Quick test checklist in UI:

- Go to sidebar `Mission Controls` → choose attack type/IP → click `Launch Attack`
- Confirm metric cards increase (`Total`, `Blocked`, attack type counters)
- In `🎛️ Command Center`, verify:
  - Live log shows the new event
  - Blocked IP appears
  - Payload inspector shows payload + defense action
- In `🧠 Threat Intel`, verify CERT-In/NVD advisory cards render
- In `🌍 Global Attack Map`, verify map appears with attacker markers
- In `📈 Threat Analytics`, verify threat profile table and bars update
- In `📦 Response & Reports`, click `Generate PDF Report` and then `Download Latest Incident Report`

Optional real traffic test (separate terminal):

```bash
python -m http.server 8080
python attack_simulator.py --type all --target http://localhost:8080
```

Then refresh the dashboard and confirm attacks are reflected.

If map/PDF parts fail, usually it is missing packages—run:
- `pip install folium reportlab`

If you want, I can also give you a strict 2-minute “judge demo script” you can read line-by-line during presentation.

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 9.4s)

_Thinking:_



Perfect — this error is normal on Arch (PEP 668).  
Your system Python blocks global `pip install`, and `streamlit` isn’t found because you’re not inside the project venv.

Use this (recommended):

```bash
cd "/home/izumi/Desktop/Everything i make/Cyber_Project"
source venv/bin/activate.fish
python -m pip install -r requirements.txt
streamlit run dashboard.py
```

If `streamlit` still says unknown, run it directly from the venv:

```bash
./venv/bin/streamlit run dashboard.py
```

Quick verify commands:

```bash
which python
which pip
which streamlit
```

They should point to `.../Cyber_Project/venv/bin/...`.

If your existing `venv` is broken, rebuild it:

```bash
cd "/home/izumi/Desktop/Everything i make/Cyber_Project"
python -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate.fish
python -m pip install --upgrade pip
python -m pip install -r requirements.txt
streamlit run dashboard.py
```

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 12.9s)

_Thinking:_



Great question — this is exactly the right mindset.

This project helps you win **if you present it as a complete cyber defense platform**, not just a dashboard.

**Why this is useful (to judges)**
- It detects real attack patterns (SQLi/XSS/LFI/CMDi), not fake random alerts.
- It auto-responds (blocks attacker IP), so it’s not “monitor-only.”
- It maps attacks to CVEs + CERT-In advisories, so it adds threat intelligence context.
- It gives decision support (threat scoring, geo map, incident report, alerting).
- It works in demo mode without root/cloud, so it’s reliable on stage.

**How this can win nationals**
Judges usually score: innovation + technical depth + real-world impact + demo quality.

Map your pitch to that:

- **Innovation:** “We unified detection + response + threat intel + reporting in one console.”
- **Technical depth:** packet/rule engine, auto-block pipeline, scoring model, CVE/CERT integration.
- **Impact:** SOC teams save time; SMEs get low-cost protection; faster incident response.
- **Demo quality:** your UI now shows everything live with interactive flows and artifacts (map/report).

**Your winning demo flow (3-4 mins)**
1. Start clean dashboard (“all secure”).
2. Launch one SQLi attack.
3. Show log entry appears instantly + IP auto-blocked.
4. Jump to CVE/CERT tab: “matched active vulnerability intelligence.”
5. Show map marker appears.
6. Show threat score rises for attacker.
7. Click “Generate PDF report” + show downloadable incident report.
8. End with: “From attack to response to compliance report in under 30 seconds.”

**What to say in one killer line**
“We built an autonomous blue-team copilot for web attacks — detect, contain, explain, and report in real time.”

**To maximize winning chances tonight**
- Add one “business KPI” card: `Mean Time To Detect`, `Mean Time To Block`.
- Prepare one slide with architecture + one with impact numbers.
- Rehearse a no-fail offline demo (use simulator only).
- Keep 2 backup recordings in case internet fails.

If you want, I can now write your exact **national-level 90-second pitch script** + **judge Q&A answers** (the hard questions like false positives, scalability, and deployment).

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 19.5s)

_Thinking:_



You built a **full-stack cyber defense demo platform** called AutoShield AI — not just a UI.

**What you have made**
- A working security pipeline: **attack simulation -> detection -> auto-response -> intelligence enrichment -> analytics -> reporting**.
- A live Streamlit SOC-style console that connects your backend modules into one interface.
- A project that can run locally without paid APIs/cloud, which is huge for hackathon reliability.

**Current features (exactly)**
- **Attack Detection Engine** (`scapy_engine.py`)
  - Detects `SQLi`, `XSS`, `LFI`, `CMDi` via rule/signature matching.
  - Logs severity, confidence, payload snippet, matched rules, CVE hints.
  - Supports simulated attacks (demo-safe), plus sniffing mode when possible.
- **Auto Defense** (`auto_block.py`)
  - Auto-block logic for malicious IPs.
  - `iptables` blocking in root mode, in-memory blocking fallback in demo mode.
  - Rate-limit based escalation, unblock + auto-expiry.
- **Threat Intelligence**
  - CVE enrichment from NVD + fallback (`cve_lookup.py`).
  - CERT-In/NVD advisory feed + attack-to-advisory matching (`certin_feed.py`).
- **Alerting** (`alert_system.py`)
  - Twilio WhatsApp + SMTP email alert pipeline.
  - Severity threshold + cooldown/throttle logic.
- **Geo Visualization** (`attack_map.py`)
  - Interactive world map of attack sources with severity visualization.
- **Threat Scoring** (`threat_score.py`)
  - Per-IP risk scoring and labels based on attack behavior features.
- **Reporting** (`report_generator.py`)
  - One-click PDF incident report for compliance/forensics.
- **Unified Dashboard** (`dashboard.py`)
  - Multi-tab command center, interactive controls, metrics, logs, payload inspector, intel, map, analytics, alerts, report download.

**How useful this is in real life**
- Very useful as a **SOC training/demo/PoC tool** for SMEs, colleges, hackathon evaluators.
- Demonstrates a realistic security workflow end-to-end.
- Helps explain cyber incidents to technical + non-technical stakeholders fast.

Now the brutal honesty:

**What is strong enough for nationals**
- End-to-end integration (many teams fail here).
- Live interactivity with visible response actions.
- Multiple security layers (detection + defense + intel + reporting).
- Good demo storytelling potential.

**What is weak right now (and judges may attack)**
- Detection is mostly **rule-based**, not truly ML-trained despite ML wording.
- Mostly demo traffic, not robust production packet processing at scale.
- No rigorous benchmark: false positive rate, precision/recall, latency, throughput.
- Limited adversarial robustness/evasion handling.
- No hardened deployment architecture (auth, RBAC, distributed collectors, SIEM integration).
- Some modules are “best-effort integration” rather than enterprise-grade reliability.

**Can it win NATIONAL level?**
- **Yes, possible** — if judged as hackathon innovation + execution demo.
- **No, not guaranteed** if competing against deep-research or production-grade cybersecurity teams.
- Realistically: this is a **strong finalist-level prototype**.  
  To become a likely winner, you need:
  1. Measured results (accuracy + response-time metrics),
  2. Clear novelty claim,
  3. Tight live demo + strong pitch framing,
  4. Honest “roadmap to production” slide.

If you want, I’ll give you a **judge-proof positioning script**: exactly how to pitch this so weaknesses sound like deliberate engineering tradeoffs, not gaps.

def _handle_event(event: dict, engine: AutoShieldEngine, blocker: BlockManager, threat_engine):
    if not event:
        return

    blocker.auto_respond(event)
    engine.mark_blocked(event.get("src_ip", "0.0.0.0"))
    profile = threat_engine.ingest(event)
    event["threat_profile"] = profile
    event["certin_matches"] = match_attack_to_certin(event.get("attack_type", ""), event.get("payload_snip", ""))
    event["alert_result"] = fire_alert(event)
```

243: 
244: def _handle_event(
245:     event: dict, engine: AutoShieldEngine, blocker: BlockManager, threat_engine
246: ):
247:     if not event:
248:         return
249: 
250:     blocker.auto_respond(event)
251:     engine.mark_blocked(event.get("src_ip", "0.0.0.0"))
252:     profile = threat_engine.ingest(event)
253:     event["threat_profile"] = profile
254:     event["certin_matches"] = match_attack_to_certin(
255:         event.get("attack_type", ""), event.get("payload_snip", "")
256:     )
257:     event["alert_result"] = fire_alert(event)
258: 
259:     st.session_state.last_attack = event
260:     st.session_state.selected_cve_type = event.get("attack_type", "SQLi")

  "patchText": "*** Begin Patch\n*** Update File: /home/izumi/Desktop/Everything i make/Cyber_Project/dashboard.py\n@@\n def _handle_event(\n     event: dict, engine: AutoShieldEngine, blocker: BlockManager, threat_engine\n ):\n@@\n     st.session_state.alert_history = st.session_state.alert_history[-80:]\n     sync_log(engine)\n+\n+\n+def _run_detector_benchmark() -> dict:\n+    detector = AttackDetector()\n+\n+    samples = [\n+        (\"GET /login?user=' OR 1=1 --&pass=x HTTP/1.1\", \"SQLi\"),\n+        (\"GET /search?q=<script>alert(1)</script> HTTP/1.1\", \"XSS\"),\n+        (\"GET /f?file=../../../../etc/passwd HTTP/1.1\", \"LFI\"),\n+        (\"GET /ping?host=8.8.8.8;cat /etc/shadow HTTP/1.1\", \"CMDi\"),\n+        (\"GET /products?id=1 UNION SELECT username,password FROM users-- HTTP/1.1\", \"SQLi\"),\n+        (\"GET /profile?name=<img src=x onerror=alert('x')> HTTP/1.1\", \"XSS\"),\n+        (\"GET /view?template=php://filter/convert.base64-encode/resource=/etc/passwd HTTP/1.1\", \"LFI\"),\n+        (\"GET /exec?cmd=id|whoami HTTP/1.1\", \"CMDi\"),\n+        (\"GET /home HTTP/1.1\", \"BENIGN\"),\n+        (\"GET /about?tab=team HTTP/1.1\", \"BENIGN\"),\n+        (\"POST /api/order HTTP/1.1 body=qty=2&item=book\", \"BENIGN\"),\n+        (\"GET /docs?q=python+streamlit HTTP/1.1\", \"BENIGN\"),\n+    ]\n+\n+    labels = [\"SQLi\", \"XSS\", \"LFI\", \"CMDi\", \"BENIGN\"]\n+    cm = {a: {p: 0 for p in labels} for a in labels}\n+\n+    for payload, actual in samples:\n+        pred_event = detector.classify(payload)\n+        predicted = pred_event.get(\"attack_type\") if pred_event else \"BENIGN\"\n+        cm[actual][predicted] += 1\n+\n+    total = len(samples)\n+    correct = sum(cm[l][l] for l in labels)\n+    accuracy = correct / total if total else 0.0\n+\n+    tp = sum(cm[label][label] for label in [\"SQLi\", \"XSS\", \"LFI\", \"CMDi\"])\n+    fp = 0\n+    fn = 0\n+    for lbl in [\"SQLi\", \"XSS\", \"LFI\", \"CMDi\"]:\n+        fp += sum(cm[a][lbl] for a in labels if a != lbl)\n+        fn += sum(cm[lbl][p] for p in labels if p != lbl)\n+\n+    precision = tp / (tp + fp) if (tp + fp) else 0.0\n+    recall = tp / (tp + fn) if (tp + fn) else 0.0\n+    f1 = (\n+        (2 * precision * recall / (precision + recall))\n+        if (precision + recall)\n+        else 0.0\n+    )\n+\n+    benign_total = sum(cm[\"BENIGN\"].values())\n+    benign_fp = benign_total - cm[\"BENIGN\"][\"BENIGN\"]\n+    fpr = benign_fp / benign_total if benign_total else 0.0\n+\n+    return {\n+        \"total_samples\": total,\n+        \"accuracy\": round(accuracy, 4),\n+        \"precision\": round(precision, 4),\n+        \"recall\": round(recall, 4),\n+        \"f1\": round(f1, 4),\n+        \"false_positive_rate\": round(fpr, 4),\n+        \"confusion_matrix\": cm,\n+    }\n+\n+\n+def _render_judge_status(current_tab: str):\n+    if not st.session_state.judge_mode:\n+        return\n+\n+    steps = [\n+        \"Launch SQLi with critical pattern\",\n+        \"Launch XSS with medium confidence\",\n+        \"Launch LFI with critical severity\",\n+        \"Launch CMDi with immediate block\",\n+    ]\n+    current = st.session_state.judge_step_idx\n+    elapsed = max(0, int(time.time() - st.session_state.judge_started_at))\n+    st.markdown(\n+        f\"\"\"\n+        <div class=\"panel\" style=\"border-color:#2b7f4d;background:rgba(25,60,40,0.35);margin-bottom:10px;\">\n+          <b style=\"color:#2dd4bf;\">Judge Mode Active</b><br/>\n+          <small style=\"color:#93a6b7;\">Tab: {current_tab} | Elapsed: {elapsed}s | Step: {current}/{len(steps)}</small><br/>\n+          <small style=\"color:#93a6b7;\">Next: {steps[current] if current < len(steps) else 'Completed. Show map + report.'}</small>\n+        </div>\n+        \"\"\",\n+        unsafe_allow_html=True,\n+    )\n*** End Patch"
}

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 9.0s)

Perfect — done. I implemented the “next serious tier” upgrades you asked for.

What I added (for actual hackathon advantage):

- `Judge Mode` (auto 90-second style sequence)
  - Start/Stop controls in sidebar.
  - Automatically injects a staged sequence of attacks every few seconds.
  - Live progress/status banner across tabs.
  - Ends automatically after the scripted run.
  - File: `dashboard.py`

- `Role-based views` (Analyst / SOC Lead / Executive)
  - Persona selector in sidebar.
  - Active persona context panel under KPI cards so you can tailor your narration to judges.
  - File: `dashboard.py`

- `Detector Benchmark panel` (hard metrics, not just visuals)
  - Added synthetic labeled evaluation set and benchmark runner.
  - Computes and displays:
    - Accuracy
    - Precision
    - Recall
    - F1
    - False Positive Rate
    - Confusion matrix
  - Triggered from sidebar: `Run Detector Benchmark`.
  - Shows in Analytics tab.
  - File: `dashboard.py`

- `Attack event intelligence enrichment` (already requested in previous step, now leveraged)
  - `event_id`, `detection_source`, OWASP mapping, MITRE mapping, and playbook notes integrated into event lifecycle.
  - Executive snapshot uses this.
  - File: `scapy_engine.py` + `dashboard.py`

- `KPI/ops improvements`
  - MTTD / MTTB / response-chain KPI state handling kept and displayed.
  - Judge mode now re-runs automatically while active so it feels “live”.
  - File: `dashboard.py`

Validation:
- Syntax check passed:
  - `python -m py_compile dashboard.py scapy_engine.py`

Files updated:
- `dashboard.py`
- `scapy_engine.py`

How to use immediately:
1. Launch app: `source venv/bin/activate.fish && streamlit run dashboard.py`

   - choose role view,

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 12.1s)

Awesome ask — I’ve now upgraded it toward true **real-time operations** and improved the overall UX/flow significantly.

What I improved right now:

- Real-time event processing pipeline in `dashboard.py`
  - Added pending-event processor that continuously picks up new `PENDING` events and auto-runs full response (block + threat score + advisory match + alert).
  - Added processed-event tracking to avoid duplicate handling.
  - Works for both simulated events and live sniffed events.

- Stronger live behavior controls
  - Auto-refresh is now **ON by default**.
  - Added configurable refresh interval slider (`1–10s`).
  - Added stream status indicators showing:
    - Live sniff vs simulation mode
    - Refresh ON/OFF
    - Count of processed events

- Live sniff toggle in UI
  - Added `Live sniff mode` toggle in sidebar.
  - Starts/stops engine from dashboard (with graceful fallback handling).

- Better operational observability
  - Added “LIVE STREAM ACTIVE” chip near top status.
  - Payload inspector now includes event metadata (event id, source, OWASP).
  - Map tab now also shows recent attacker sequence table (latest 10 events).

- Better state hygiene
  - Reset now also clears processed event IDs to keep runs clean.

- Kept prior upgrades intact
  - Judge Mode, Autopilot, benchmark panel, KPI cards, role views, threat intel, reporting.

Validation:
- Syntax verified:
  - `python -m py_compile dashboard.py scapy_engine.py` passed.

Files updated:
- `dashboard.py`
- (previously enhanced) `scapy_engine.py`

How to test “real-time” quickly:

1. Start app and keep auto-refresh ON (2s interval).
2. Turn on `Live sniff mode` (if privileges/scapy support available).
3. In another terminal run:
   - `python attack_simulator.py --type all --target http://localhost:8080`
4. Watch:
   - log rows appear and transition through response pipeline
   - blocked list update
   - KPI and analytics update live
   - map and sequence table refresh

If you want, next I can implement **WebSocket-style push updates** (no polling refresh delay) by adding a lightweight event bus/thread-safe queue integration.
