## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 11.9s)

You’re absolutely right — those `CONNECTION_REFUSED` runs mean your simulator had nowhere to send HTTP traffic, so it looked “dead.” I fixed this in a way that makes your demo feel live even when no server is up.

What I changed to make it genuinely better:

- Added real-time CLI event stream bridge
  - `attack_simulator.py` now writes every attack as JSONL events to `/tmp/autoshield_event_stream.jsonl`.
  - `dashboard.py` now ingests that stream continuously and converts it into live dashboard incidents.
  - Result: your dashboard updates in real time from CLI runs even if target server is down.

- Added fallback “emit-only” simulator mode
  - New simulator flag: `--emit-only`
  - This streams attacks without making HTTP calls, so no `CONNECTION_REFUSED` spam.
  - Great for stage demos and judge mode reliability.

- Added stream controls in dashboard
  - Sidebar toggle: `CLI stream ingest` ON/OFF
  - `Reset Stream Offset` button
  - Stream cursor tracking shown in Command Center status panel
  - You now see if stream ingestion is actively moving.

- Improved live status visibility
  - Command Center status now shows:
    - Simulation vs live sniff mode
    - CLI ingest state
    - Refresh state
    - Processed event count
    - Stream cursor offset
  - Added quick launch command block in Response tab for operators/judges.

- Kept previous upgrades and integrated them with stream ingestion
  - KPI cards, benchmark, judge mode, role view, map, threat analytics, reports.

Files updated:
- `attack_simulator.py`
- `dashboard.py`
- (already enhanced) `scapy_engine.py`

How to run now (best demo path):

- Terminal 1:
  - `source venv/bin/activate.fish`
  - `streamlit run dashboard.py`

- Terminal 2 (reliable, no backend server needed):
  - `source venv/bin/activate.fish`
  - `python attack_simulator.py --type all --emit-only`

Optional real HTTP path:
- Start local server first:
  - `python -m http.server 8080`
- Then run:
  - `python attack_simulator.py --type all --target http://localhost:8080`

Why you saw that warning:
- `RequestsDependencyWarning` = your global Python packages are mixed versions.
- It won’t break the demo flow, but for clean output use venv:
  - `source venv/bin/activate.fish`
  - run commands from there.

If you want, next I can make the UI auto-highlight **new incoming events** with short-lived row glow + “new” badges so it feels even more real-time on stage.

754:         atype, ip = judge_sequence[st.session_state.judge_step_idx]
755:         ev = engine.simulate_attack(atype, src_ip=ip)
756:         _handle_event(ev, engine, blocker, threat_engine)
757:         st.session_state.judge_step_idx += 1
758: 
759:     if st.session_state.judge_step_idx >= len(judge_sequence):
760:         st.session_state.judge_mode = False
761:     else:
762:         time.sleep(1)
763:         st.rerun()
764: 
765: m1, m2, m3, m4, m5, m6, m7 = st.columns(7)
766: metric_card(m1, total_attacks, "Total Attacks", "#62c0ff")
767: metric_card(m2, blocked_count, "Blocked", "#26d07c")
768: metric_card(m3, sqli_count, "SQLi", "#ff7d73")
769: metric_card(m4, xss_count, "XSS", "#ffcc66")
770: metric_card(m5, lfi_count, "LFI", "#9ea8ff")
771: metric_card(m6, cmdi_count, "CMDi", "#ffab66")
772: metric_card(m7, max_threat_score, "Top Threat Score", "#2dd4bf")
773: 
774: k1, k2, k3, k4 = st.columns(4)
775: metric_card(
776:     k1, f"{st.session_state.kpi.get('last_mttd_ms', 0)} ms", "Last MTTD", "#62c0ff"
777: )
778: metric_card(
779:     k2, f"{st.session_state.kpi.get('last_mttb_ms', 0)} ms", "Last MTTB", "#26d07c"
780: )
781: metric_card(
782:     k3,
783:     f"{st.session_state.kpi.get('last_response_chain_ms', 0)} ms",
784:     "Response Chain",
785:     "#f8b84d",
786: )
787: metric_card(
788:     k4,
789:     f"{st.session_state.kpi.get('best_confidence', 0)}%",
790:     "Peak Confidence",
791:     "#ff9f5a",
792: )
793: 
794: st.markdown(
795:     f"""
796:     <div class="panel" style="margin-top:8px;">
797:       Active persona: <b>{st.session_state.role_view}</b>
798:       {"| Focus: tactical triage and payload evidence" if st.session_state.role_view == "Analyst" else ""}
799:       {"| Focus: risk posture, response velocity, and operations" if st.session_state.role_view == "SOC Lead" else ""}
